January 3, 2000


HEADLINE: Late Night Political Humor.


BODY:

Jay Leno: "Presidential candidate Gary Bauer -- you know him, the little guy there? I think he usually sits on Reggie White's knee. He says the Vermont Supreme Court's decision to recognize gay couples is worse than terrorism. Really? Wouldn't you rather have a gay couple living next door than a terrorist? At least his yard would be nicer, wouldn't it?" 

Jay Leno: "According to the National Enquirer -- listen to this -- Linda Tripp recently had a face-lift. And the bad news, the doctor who.gave her the face-lift got a hernia."

Jay Leno: "A woman artist, she uses her breasts to paint with. She dips them in paint and then she presses them on a canvas. And she's doing quite well. In fact, today Clinton asked her to paint his official White House portrait, yeah. Clinton also offered to help clean the brushes, which I thought was nice."

Conan O'Brien: "George W. Bush had a quote today. He said that if elected President -- this was his big statement -- if elected President, he would not object if a guest wanted to light up and smoke at a state dinner. That was his statement. That's what he said. That's right. Yeah, Bush says he only hopes they have the courtesy not to hog the crack pipes."

Conan O'Brien: "Also in politics today, Minnesota Governor Jesse Ventura said he will not.support Pat Buchanan in his bid for the nomination in the Reform Party. Not going to support him. He had a reason. Ventura explained, 'I'm sorry, but Buchanan's ridiculous views conflict with my ridiculous views. '"

Conan O'Brien: "It was reported today that in the past few months Linda Tripp, we all know and love her -- this is what she's had -- she's had a nose job, a chin tuck, neck reduction, and liposuction. She's had all of that done. Yeah. True story. Not only that, not only that, she is now taping conversations in Dolby stereo."

David Letterman: "People are going crazy celebrating early. In fact, down in Washington, President Clinton spent the entire day playing with a noisemaker. . I believe her name is Rhonda."

Craig Kilborn: "According to The National Enquirer, Linda Tripp had a plastic surgery makeover to improve her looks. And that's good. Now, after the surgery, Linda Tripp's doctor upgraded her condition to 'very unattractive.'"

Craig Kilborn: "Linda's operation included a chin tuck, a facial peel, and what we call a snout job."

Craig Kilborn: "Monica Lewinsky.has some Jenny Craig commercials she's doing. . Monica has opened up and said the reason she finally decided get help with her weight was she looked down and realized she couldn't see the President's feet."

Craig Kilborn: "Preparations almost complete in Times Square. . One thousand cops have been assigned to protect government buildings and three secret service guys are guarding the Mayor's hairpiece."

Jay Leno: "I can't wait to see how the neighbors react when Bill's stuff starts showing up, you know, all the stuff from Arkansas, the velveteen Elvis paintings. You know what I'm saying? The Astroturf for the porch, you know, the car up on blocks in the front yard." 

Jay Leno: "To help with the move, Hillary's opponent, Mayor Rudy Giuliani -- you know, they're supposed to be archrivals -- sent over some cardboard boxes to help her move. Now, he did. He did. Unfortunately, he took them from homeless people who were living in them at the time."

Jay Leno: "You know what's going on tonight? President Clinton is flying up to stay in the house. Hillary and Bill are gonna spend their first night in the new house together. I understand President Clinton's a little nervous. Well, you remember how it was the first time you slept with someone. You don't know what they like."

Jay Leno: "And in his new budget, President Clinton now proposing $10 million to help develop smart gun technology. Are you familiar with this? With smart gun technology, the gun will only work if it's handled by you, not if it's held by another. If it's handled by you, it will work. If it's held by another person, it won't go off. And today, Hillary says she wants the same technology installed in the President's pants."

Jay Leno: "President Clinton was in West Virginia yesterday with Israel and Syrian leaders for those Middle East peace talks. Then he's heading down to Atlanta for peace talks with Jane Fonda and Ted Turner."

Jay Leno: "Who would have thought the man with the most stable marriage at CNN would be Larry King?"

Jay Leno: "Did you all watch Monica Lewinsky on 'Larry King' the other night? Yeah, she told Larry she's seeing a therapist now. Just hope his wife doesn't find out."

Jay Leno: "She also said on 'Larry King' the other night that she'll always have a small room in her heart for President Clinton. Today, President Clinton called and said, 'I'd like to reserve that room for the weekend.'"

Jay Leno: "For a woman who says she's not a media hound, she is doing a lot of interviews. She is on everything. This could be the first time she's ever got chapped lips just from talking."

Jay Leno: "Boris 'Buy Me a Drink' Yeltsin. Yeltsin, you know, he's a private citizen now. He announced today he would like to continue working for the government, for the Russian government, in some capacity. Maybe something like Ambassador to Margaritaville."

Jay Leno: "This woman in New Mexico has come out of a 16-year coma. Did you read about this? Woman had a baby, went into a coma, just came out of it. 16 years in a coma. And I guess she's doing okay. Doctors told her to take it easy. They told her, take walks, and, for God's sakes, avoid watching any of the Al Gore-Bill Bradley debates. They said that could plunge her right back in again."

Conan O'Brien: "Tonight, Hillary Clinton will spend her first night in her house in upstate New York. And this prompted President Clinton to ask, 'Is it too late to change my New Year's resolution?'"

David Letterman: "Top Ten Ways The White House Is Different Now That Hillary Has Moved Out: 10. President no longer sleeping alone. 9. Faucets in master bedroom now dispense scented message oil and gravy. 8. Forget dress down Friday - now all-nude Friday and pantsless Monday through Thursday. 7. Volumes of Hillary fan mail redirected to new house. 6. Hillary no longer writing volumes of fan mail to herself. 5. No pressure to cuddle. 4. Token male intern transferred out. 3. Oval office covered with 'Vote Giuliani' posters. 2. Women's soccer team no longer has to win World Cup to spend night at White House. 1. Menorah taken off living room mantle."

David Letterman: "Alan Greenspan has been convinced to stay another term as the Chairman of the Fed, you know. He said he'd do it under one condition: he wants in on some of that hot intern action."

David Letterman: "Hillary Clinton moved from Washington to her house here in New York. She and Janet Reno, they swung by Ryder and moved themselves."

David Letterman: "Hillary spent the day unloading boxes, and boxes, and boxes of personal stuff, or as we call it, evidence."

David Letterman: "Now her husband, Bill Clinton, says that when he's out of the White House, he'd like to move back to Arkansas and run for Senate, as well. So, you have Clinton, Bill, living in Arkansas, Hillary living in New York. And I'm thinking, I hope this doesn't put a strain on their marriage."

David Letterman: "Boris Yeltsin had a couple of stiff belts and resigned on New Year's Eve. And we're learning more and more about his successor, the acting president of Russia, Vladimir Putin. He has a black belt in Karate. And I thought, that's a coincidence right there, because Bill Clinton, our President, has a black belt. It's usually down around his ankles, but that's not the point."

Bill Maher: "Ted Kennedy endorsed Al Gore. Gore was so excited, he lost it and claimed that he invented the liver transplant."

Bill Maher: "Pat Buchanan said he's expecting a big upsurge now because with Y2K put behind us, his constituents are now free to leave their bunkers."

Bill Maher: "In West Virginia, they are trying to solve the Middle East peace problem. The negotiators from Israel and Syria -- President Clinton was there yesterday, trying to encourage them, trying to get these guys to finally make a lasting peace in the Middle East. It's very tough to get these negotiators to renounce violence, because if you do, first of all, if kills any chance of ever dating Jennifer Lopez."

Craig Kilborn: "Hillary Clinton is planning to spend her very first night in her new home in suburban Chappaqua, New York. Tonight, Bill Clinton is planning to spend the night with a band, a bathtub full of margaritas and 45 waitresses from Hooter's."

Craig Kilborn: "According to the movers, packing up the President's things was simple. Everything he cherishes fits neatly into a humidor."

Craig Kilborn: "Mrs. Clinton isn't planning to spend too much time setting up their home because it's a matter of days before Bill wrecks it."

Craig Kilborn: "A McDonald's ad running in Hong Kong has angered officials from China's army because it shows a boy offering french fries to a soldier. . This is the second time McDonald's has offended China. In an ad last year Ronald McDonald was seen making an illegal campaign contribution to Al Gore."

Craig Kilborn: "Media mogul Ted Turner and actress Jane Fonda say they are separating. Or, as it's called these days, moving to Chappaqua."

Craig Kilborn: "Stunned by the news, President Clinton called Jane Fonda to say, 'Come on over. Hillary's gone.'"

HEADLINE: Last Laughs: Late Night Political Humor.


BODY:

Jay Leno: "I'm sure you know by now, Bill and Hillary Clinton have moved into their new home in the small community of Chappaqua, New York. . You know, 'Chappaqua' is an old Indian word meaning 'place to dump the wife.'"

Jay Leno: "We got Hillary a housewarming gift. Can't go wrong with a map of New York. I think she might need that." 

Jay Leno: "It's funny, today a reporter asked President Clinton, 'How does it feel to spend the night in a strange house?' He said, 'Oh, hell, I do that at least four nights a week.'"

Jay Leno: "Did you see this on the news, they showed Hillary and Bill walking around their backyard, holding hands. Did you see that? You know, it's kind of like that footage at the zoo, where they put the two pandas together. You know they're not sexually attracted. You just hope something will happen. You know, they put them in the cage, they walk around. 'Hey look, maybe they'll do something. Oh, no, I guess not. The male does not seem interested.'"

Jay Leno: "Clinton told reporters that he and Hillary stayed up late the other night unpacking boxes. And they discovered possessions they hadn't seen in 17 years. Like every time they'd pull something out of a box, Hillary would say, 'Oh, my God, I remember who you were cheating on me with when we first got this item.'"

Jay Leno: "That's got to be strange, don't you think? Opening boxes and seeing things you haven't seen in 17 years. Then they went upstairs, got undressed for bed and the same thing happened. They saw things they hadn't seen for 17 years."

Jay Leno: "A lot of cynics are saying the Clintons are using this as an excuse to engage in a trial separation. You know what that is, a trial separation? That's when they're separated, but stay married so they can't testify against each other at their trial."

Jay Leno: "And Al Gore really went after Bill Bradley the other night. Whoo! Did you see that? He said Bill Bradley's health care plan will leave the American people 'high and dry.' I always like that. You always hear politicians use that expression, that somebody will leave the people 'high and dry.' You never hear them say somebody will leave them 'low and wet.' Okay, maybe Clinton, he's the only one."

Jay Leno: "I guess the first primary is next month in New Hampshire. In a few weeks, you know, you'll see the number of candidates start to dwindle down. You know, when you watch this political race, it's kind of like keeping a tank of tropical fish. You know what I mean? Every once in a while you look in, you count them. There's not as many as there were before. Until there's only one left and he's really fat and mean, you know?"

Jay Leno: "And yesterday, to protest the decision to return that 6-year-old boy back to Cuba, a large group of Cuban refugees in Miami intentionally drove very slowly on the freeway. Drove slowly around town, blocking traffic. So you had thousands of immigrants driving really slow in the fast lane blocking traffic -- or as we call that in LA -- rush hour."

Jay Leno: "Bad news today for Linda Tripp. Oh, boy. Did you hear about this? Oh gosh. Today her body rejected her new face."

Jay Leno: "As I'm sure you know, Linda Tripp underwent extensive plastic surgery and liposuction. I don't know.just because you put an awning on the outhouse doesn't make it a guest room, okay?"

Jay Leno: (The theme from "The Hillary No-Billy":) "Come and listen to my story about a girl named Hil, who was sick and tired of that cheatin' no good Bill. Got so fed up with the women on his lap that she loaded up the truck and bought a Yankee cap -- New York that is. Senate seat up for grabs. Well, the next thing you know she's bought a brand-new house, trying to put some distance from that no-good horny louse. Now Hillary is out on the campaign trail, while Bill is back home chasing intern tail -- girls that is. DNA, Jenny Craig."

Conan O'Brien: "President Clinton was in New York all this week getting settled into his brand-new home in the suburbs. And yesterday -- true story -- two of his neighbors dropped off bottles of champagne. Isn't that nice? I thought that was sweet. Not only that, but three other neighbors dropped off restraining orders."

Conan O'Brien: "Jenny Craig franchises in Wisconsin and Iowa are refusing to air the Monica Lewinsky ads because they say Monica is not a person to look up to. That's right. That's what they said. True story. And this is the weird part: Monica actually agreed, and said, 'You know, usually, I'm the one looking up.'"

Craig Kilborn: "Donald Trump today told reporters there was, quote, a very good possibility he would announce he's running for president next month and he said if he runs he will commit $100 million of his own money, $20 million towards the campaign and the rest for something The Donald calls 'tang.'"

Craig Kilborn: "Last night Republican presidential hopefuls Bush, McCain, Forbes, Hatch, and Bauer all competed on TV's hottest new game show, 'Who Wants To Be A President?'"

Craig Kilborn: "The new issue of People magazine has scooped its competitors with exclusive pictures of Linda Tripp's plastic surgery. She had an eye job, neck tuck, and skin peel and while she was under, doctors figured she might as well get spayed."

Craig Kilborn: "Boris Yeltsin and Yasser Arafat.attended an Orthodox Christian service yesterday. Between the two of them, needless to say, everyone got bombed."

10. Fun to hear White House spokesman use phrase 'road rage'
